Exhibit B


**Price Proposal**


Respondent: __Presidio___________________________


Solution Proposed: Armis Centrix Asset Management*_


*Armis for Asset Management consolidates asset data into one complete, de-duplicated and authoritative
asset map. Creates a complete asset inventory of all asset types from the ground to the cloud ensuring
the entire attack surface is both defended and managed in real time. Complete visibility into assets
behaviors and risk management based on business context, threat and vulnerability insights and the
collective intelligence of billions of assets monitored by the Armis Asset Intelligence Engine. Asset
minimum 2000 per tenant. Network ports also known as collectors.


Tier 1 - includes up to 2 network ports
Tier 2 - includes up to 4 network ports
Tier 3 - includes up to 8 network ports
Tier 4 - includes up to 16 network ports
Tier 5 - includes up to 32 network ports
Tier 6 - includes up to 64 network ports
Tier 7 - includes up to 64 network ports


Service Category: Service Category 2: Network-Based Asset Discovery

**Price Proposal**

Respondent: _Armis, Inc._______________________

Solution Proposed: _Armis VIPR Pro*_________________

*VIPR Pro empowers enterprises with a unified platform for technology risk prioritization and resolution
lifecycle management. VIPR Professional automates risk prioritization and orientation through
consolidation and contextualization of detection tool findings, through asset intelligence and configurable
risk assessment. It then automates ticketing and task routing across multiple instances of the same
workflow tools. Asset minimum 2000 per tenant.

Service Category: Service Category 13: Vulnerability Assessment and Management

# **Attachment B** **Price Proposal**


Respondent shall provide a Price Proposal for each Solution proposed for a given Service Category.
Pricing proposed shall be used by the Department to evaluate the Respondents Solution. Provide Price
Proposals in a PDF file. **Provision of a Price Proposal is a mandatory responsiveness requirement** .

**Mandatory Requirements** . On each Price Proposal submitted, Respondent shall, at a minimum: (1)
state the applicable Service Category, (2) provide the name of the Solution proposed, and (3) provide
pricing information for the proposed Solution for both the initial and renewal term. If no renewal pricing is
proposed, Respondent affirms its submitted pricing for the initial term shall be applicable to any renewal
terms.

The Department prefers that Respondents pricing:


1) Provides not-to-exceed pricing for initial term and renewal term of the Solution; and


2) Provides Tiered Pricing, where greater numbers of units purchased provide discounted pricing.


Provision of not-to-exceed pricing and tiered pricing is not a mandatory requirement, but will result in the
Respondent receiving a higher Price Proposal score, as further explained in Attachment C, Evaluation
Criteria.

Add-On Services ( **OPTIONAL** ): Respondent may include the names, descriptions, and prices for AddOn services for the proposed Solution in its Price Proposal. If the Solution has separate charges for
implementation, integration, or other start-up costs, these must be included in the Add-On Services
portion of the Respondents Price Proposal. For each Add-On Service proposed, Respondent shall
describe the Add-On Service. Descriptions for each Add-On Service should be a maximum of 250 words.
Failure to enter a name, description, and price for each proposed Add-On Service may result in that AddOn Service not being made available on the Term Contract, if awarded. If the Renewal Term Add-On
Services is not provided, Respondent affirms pricing for the Initial Term shall be applicable to any renewal
terms.

The Department reserves the right to seek clarification where necessary regarding all submitted Price
Proposals.

A sample Price Proposal is provided on the following page. Respondents are encouraged to utilize the
sample to ensure that the requirements specified above are provided, but may utilize an alternative format
that contains the required information.

Digital Security Solutions

Docusign Envelope ID: 0EB12AD6-31B0-49C3-BA21-D11EB2B2577C

## **Additional Okta Solutions**


**Identity Governance**
Okta Identity Governance streamlines user access oversight by automating reviews,
certifications, and approval processes. It ensures compliance with regulations and reduces risks
by giving organizations full visibility and control over access policies.


**Workflow**
Okta Workflow is a no-code automation platform that connects identity events to IT and
business processes. It enables organizations to create custom workflows for user provisioning,
deprovisioning, and notifications without writing code, enhancing efficiency and reducing errors.


**Lifecycle Management (LCM)**
Okta LCM automates the onboarding and offboarding of users across all systems, ensuring the
right access is provisioned or revoked. It integrates seamlessly with HR systems, reducing
manual efforts and improving security.


**Device Access**
Okta Device Access secures access to enterprise resources by enforcing policies on enrolled
devices. It ensures only trusted devices can access sensitive data, bolstering endpoint security
in zero-trust environments.


**Access Gateway**
Okta Access Gateway extends modern identity capabilities to on-premise applications. It
integrates legacy systems with Okta's cloud-based authentication, enabling a hybrid approach
to identity management.


**Identity Threat Protection (ITP)**
Okta ITP safeguards against identity-based attacks by detecting and mitigating threats like
phishing and credential stuffing. It leverages contextual signals, adaptive policies, and advanced
threat intelligence.


**Identity Security Posture Management (ISPM)**
Okta ISPM provides continuous monitoring and assessment of identity configurations. It
identifies and addresses vulnerabilities to maintain a secure identity environment and align with
zero-trust principles.

gigabytes or terabytes, and operates on a subscription basis with annual or multi-year
commitments. Splunk Cloud can only be purchased by increments of 50GB, with 50GB being the
minimum. Pricing below is not to exceed pricing for Splunk Cloud w/ encryption at rest. Additional
flavors of Splunk cloud are available (commercial cloud, FedRamp or compliance (HIPPA/PCI).

Add-On Services ( **OPTIONAL** ) for **initial** term:

**Professional services -** are billed on a per-day basis. Splunk PS has created Implementation
Packages aligned to our products. Depending on the scope of a customer's license and
environment, the amount of professional services required will vary. Cost for professional services
will be billed as they are used. Each customer will be scoped according to their products, data
sources, data size, users, dashboards, reports and SOAR playbooks. These services will be
delivered remotely. If the customer requires on-site resources, travel and expense costs will be
incurred.

**Training Units -** also known as "education credits" or "training credits", are Splunk Educationspecific currency that can be used on any paid Splunk training offering.
